def key_logging():
    while True:
        try:
            presses = pyautogui.keyLogs.events()
            for event in presses:
                if str(event.type) == "mouse" or str(event.type) == "keyboard":
                    log_file.write(f'{time.time()} - {event.type} - {event.description}\n')

            print(e)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    key_logging()
